  <script lang="js">
   var app = window.app || {};
app.refreshUserCookies = (function (module) {
    var serviceUrl = "https://micuenta.lne.es/login/refresh-cookies";
    var ERROR_MAX_TRIES = 3;
    var STORAGE_KEY_REFRESHED_AT = 'nxUserCookiesLastRefreshedAt';

    var storageWrapper = {};
    if (typeof Storage === 'function') {
        storageWrapper = localStorage;
    } else {
        storageWrapper.getItem = function (name) {
            var value = '; ' + document.cookie;
            var parts = value.split('; ' + name + '=');
            if (parts.length === 2) {
                return parts.pop()
                    .split(';')
                    .shift();
            }
        };
        storageWrapper.setItem = function (name, value) {
            var expires = new Date();
            expires.setHours(2, 0, 0, 0);
            expires.setDate(expires.getDate() + 1); // Tomorrow at 02:00
            document.cookie = name + '=' + value + ';expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
        };
        storageWrapper.removeItem = function (name) {
            document.cookie = name + '=;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT';
        };
    }

    var now = new Date();
    var todayAt2 = new Date(now);
    todayAt2.setHours(2, 0, 0);

    var lastRefreshedAt = new Date(storageWrapper.getItem(STORAGE_KEY_REFRESHED_AT));
    if (!lastRefreshedAt.getTime()
        || (now > todayAt2) !== (lastRefreshedAt > todayAt2)) {

        var STORAGE_KEY_ERROR_TRY_COUNT = 'nxUserCookiesErrorTryCount-' + (todayAt2.getTime());
        var errorTryCount = parseInt(storageWrapper.getItem(STORAGE_KEY_ERROR_TRY_COUNT) || 0);
        if (errorTryCount >= ERROR_MAX_TRIES) {
            module.success = false;
            module.errorMessage = "Max tries reached for today: " + errorTryCount;
        } else {
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open('GET', serviceUrl, true);
            xhr.withCredentials = true;
            xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
                if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
                    module.refreshStauts = xhr.status;
                    module.refreshResponse = xhr.responseText;
                    module.lastRefreshedAt = lastRefreshedAt;
                    if (xhr.status === 200) {
                        module.success = true;
                        storageWrapper.setItem(STORAGE_KEY_REFRESHED_AT, now.toUTCString());
                        storageWrapper.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY_ERROR_TRY_COUNT);
                    } else {
                        module.success = false;
                        module.errorMessage = "Response status was different from 200: " + xhr.status;
                        errorTryCount++;
                        storageWrapper.setItem(STORAGE_KEY_ERROR_TRY_COUNT, errorTryCount);
                        module.errorTryCount = errorTryCount;
                    }
                }
            };
            try {
                xhr.send(null);
            } catch (e) {
            }
        }
    } else {
        module.success = true;
        module.lastRefreshedAt = lastRefreshedAt;
    }

    return module;
})(app.refreshUserCookies || {});
  </script>

        module.premiumEnabled = 1;
        module.userIsSusbcriber = !!getCookie('suscripciones');
        module.hideAdsForSubscribers = module.userIsSusbcriber && module.premiumEnabled;
        module.log = console.log.bind(console, '%c[PUBLICIDAD]', 'color:green');
        module.error = console.error.bind(console, '[PUBLICIDAD]');
        module.epiCountBiddersDone = 0;
        module.positionsDisplayedImmediately = [];
        module.positionsDisplayedAtScroll = {};
        module.positionsOmmited = [];
        module.screenWidth = screen ? screen.width : 0;
        module.device = (module.screenWidth <= 500) ? 'mobile' : 'desktop'
        module.renderQueue = (function (disableRefreshAd) {
            if (disableRefreshAd) {
                module.log('No se llamará a `googletag.pubads().refresh(ads)` porque así fue indicado en el AdMap.');
                return { push: function () {}, ready: function () {}, };
            }

            var buffer = [];
            var ready = false;

            function flush() {
                var ads = buffer.splice(0, buffer.length);
                googletag.pubads().refresh(ads);
                ads.map(function (ad) {
                    module.log('Pintando slot: ', ad.getSlotElementId());
                });
            }

            return {
                push: function (position) {
                    buffer.push(position);
                    if(ready) flush();
                },
                ready: function () {
                    module.log('Render queue ready!');
                    ready = true;
                    flush();
                }
            };
        })(module.adMap.disableRefreshAd);
        module.onLoad = (function () {
            var buffer = module.onLoad || [];
            var ready = false;

            function flush() {
                buffer.map( function (callback) { callback(module); } );
            }

            return {
                push: function (callback) {
                    buffer.push(callback);
                    if (ready) flush();
                },
                ready: function() {
                    ready = true;
                    flush();
                },
            };
        })();

        module.handleFirstAuctionEnd = function handleFirstAuctionEnd() {
            if (flags.get(flags.HANDLE_FIRST_AUCTION_END)) return;
            flags.set(flags.HANDLE_FIRST_AUCTION_END);

            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                if (typeof pbjs !== 'undefined'
                    && typeof pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync == 'function') {
                    pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
                }
                if (document.body.classList.contains('sk--photogallery')
                    && window.screen.width < 768) {
                    module.log('Omitimos el pintado de la publicidad porque estamos en una galería en móvil');
                } else {
                    flags.set(flags.PHOTOGALLERY_MOBILE);
                }
                flags.set(flags.PREBID_READY);
            });
        };

        function addCTMToVideos() {
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
                var videos = document.querySelectorAll('[data-ad-tag-url]');
                videos.forEach(function (element) {
                    var adTagUrl = element.dataset.adTagUrl;
                    if (adTagUrl) {
                        element.dataset.adTagUrl = adTagUrl + '&npa=1';
                    }
                });
            });
        }

        module.removeNonInitializedPosition = function (position) {
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-ad-position-baldomero="' + position.id + '"').forEach(function (element) {
                module.log('Se elimina el hueco de publicidad de la posición', position.id, position.slot);
                element.classList.add('baldomero');
            });
        };

        var slotIdPrefix = (screen && screen.width < 768) ? 'movil-' : 'pc-';
        module.initializePosition = function (position) {
            if (module.hideAdsForSubscribers && !position.enabledForSubscribers) {
                module.log('Se omite la siguiente posición debido a que el usuario es suscriptor.', position);
                return module.positionsOmmited.push(position);
            }

            console.group('Inicializando ' + position.slot);
            try {
                var positionId = slotIdPrefix + 'div-gpt-ad_' + position.slot;
                var adUnitPath = '/' + module.adMap.networkCode + '/' + position.type + '-' + module.adMap.adUnit;
                var slot = position.outOfPage
                    ? googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(adUnitPath, positionId)
                    : googletag.defineSlot(adUnitPath, position.sizes, positionId);
                module.log('Slot creado con id', positionId, 'y adUnit', adUnitPath, position.outOfPage ? 'como OutOfPage' : '');
                if (Array.isArray(position.mapping) && position.mapping.length) {
                    var mapping = googletag.sizeMapping();
                    position.mapping.forEach(function (map) {
                        mapping.addSize(map.key, map.value);
                    });
                    slot.defineSizeMapping(mapping.build());
                    module.log('Añadido sizeMapping a slot', position.mapping);
                }
                if (Array.isArray(position.targeting) && position.targeting.length) {
                    position.targeting.forEach(function (targeting) {
                        slot.setTargeting(targeting.key, targeting.value);
                    });
                    module.log('Añadido targeting a slot', position.targeting);
                    if (slot.getTargeting('p')[0] === slotTargetings.footer) footerAdId = positionId;
                    if (slot.getTargeting('p')[0] === slotTargetings.header) headerAdId = positionId;

                }
                slot.addService(googletag.companionAds()).addService(googletag.pubads());
                gptadslots.push(slot);
                googletag.display(slot);

                module.initializeApstagSlot(positionId, adUnitPath, position);

                if (!position.scroll) {
                    module.positionsDisplayedImmediately.push(slot);
                    module.log('La posición se pintará en cuanto el DOM esté cargado');
                } else {
                    module.positionsDisplayedAtScroll[position.scroll] = module.positionsDisplayedAtScroll[position.scroll] || [];
                    module.positionsDisplayedAtScroll[position.scroll].push(slot);
                    module.log('La posición se pintará al hacer scroll ', position.scroll);
                }

                module.log('Posición inicializada correctamente', position);
            } catch (e) {
                module.error('Error al inicializar una posición de publicidad. ' +
                    'Puede que se haya cargado dos veces el mismo slot en la página.',
                    position
                );
                module.error(e);
            }
            console.groupEnd();
        };

        module.initializeApstagSlot = function (positionId, adUnitPath, position) {
            if (position.outOfPage) return;

            var sizes = position.sizes;
            var mappingsWidths = (Object.keys(position.mappingByWidth || {})).sort().reverse();
            if (mappingsWidths.length > 0) {
                var useWidth = mappingsWidths.find(function (width) { return module.screenWidth >= width; });
                sizes = position.mappingByWidth[useWidth];
                module.log('Definiremos la posición en Apstag con los tamaños (' + useWidth + ')', sizes);
            }
            if (Array.isArray(sizes) && sizes.length > 0){
                const apsSlot = {
                    slotID: positionId,
                    slotName: adUnitPath,
                    sizes: sizes,
                };
                module.log('Posición añadida a apstagslots', apsSlot);
                apstagslots.push(apsSlot);
            }
        };

        module.displayPositionsWhenDOMReady = function displayPositions() {
            function displayAllPositions() {
                initializePubadsEventListeners();
                console.group('Pintando publicidad');
                module.log('El contenido de la página ha terminado de cargar.');

                module.log('Añadimos inmediatamente las siguientes posiciones a la cola', module.positionsDisplayedImmediately);
                module.positionsDisplayedImmediately.map(module.renderQueue.push);
                module.positionsOmmited.map(module.removeNonInitializedPosition);

                if (module.hideAdsForSubscribers) {
                    document.querySelectorAll('[data-html-ad-enabled-for-subscribers]')
                        .forEach(function (element) {
                            if (Boolean(parseInt(element.dataset.htmlAdEnabledForSubscribers))) {
                                return;
                            }
                            var parts = element.id.split('_');
                            module.removeNonInitializedPosition({ id: parts[parts.length - 1] });
                        });
                }

                Object.keys(module.positionsDisplayedAtScroll).map(function (id) {
                    var scroll = parseInt(id, 10);
                    var slots = module.positionsDisplayedAtScroll[id];
                    module.log('Escuchando el scroll de la página para pintar', scroll, slots);
                    document.addEventListener('scroll', function listener() {
                        if (document.body.scrollTop > scroll
                            || document.documentElement.scrollTop > scroll) {
                            slots.map(module.renderQueue.push);
                            document.removeEventListener('scroll', listener, true);
                        }
                    }, true);
                });
                console.groupEnd();
            }

            if (document.readyState !== 'loading') {
                displayAllPositions();
            } else {
                module.log('Escuchando cuando el contenido de la página termina de cargar para pintar publicidad.');
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', displayAllPositions);
            }
        };

        function execute() {
            module.log('Ejecutando inicialización de publicidad.');
            module.adMap.slots.map(module.initializePosition);
            module.displayPositionsWhenDOMReady();
            flags.set(flags.ADS_INITIALIZED);

            /* setTargeting cxense */
            try {
                if (localStorage.getItem('pisegs')) {
                    googletag.pubads()
                        .setTargeting('CxSegments', localStorage.getItem('pisegs'));
                }
                if (localStorage.getItem('_mo_r1')) {
                    googletag.pubads()
                        .setTargeting('r1', localStorage.getItem('_mo_r1'));
                }
                if (localStorage.getItem('_mo_r2')) {
                    googletag.pubads()
                        .setTargeting('r2', localStorage.getItem("_mo_r2"))
                }
            } catch (e) {}

            try {
                var strDat = localStorage.getItem('_mo_ipdata');
                if(strDat){
                    var objDat = JSON.parse(strDat);
                    if(objDat.cit) googletag.pubads().setTargeting("cc", objDat.cit);
                    if(objDat.zip) googletag.pubads().setTargeting("cz", objDat.zip);
                }
            } catch(e){}

            try {
                var strDat = localStorage.getItem('_mo_profile');
                if(strDat){
                    var objDat = JSON.parse(strDat);
                    if(objDat.geo) {
                        if(objDat.geo.cit) googletag.pubads().setTargeting("bc", objDat.geo.cit);
                        if(objDat.geo.zip) googletag.pubads().setTargeting("bz", objDat.geo.zip);
                    }
                }
            } catch(e){}

            var searchParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search.slice(1));
            if (searchParams.has('tagepi')) module.adMap.tags.push(searchParams.get('tagepi'));
            if (module.adMap.tags.length) googletag.pubads().setTargeting('tagepi', module.adMap.tags);
            if (module.adMap.geos.length) googletag.pubads().setTargeting('hiperlocalepi', module.adMap.geos);
            if (module.adMap.page) googletag.pubads().setTargeting('page', module.adMap.page);
            if (module.hideAdsForSubscribers) googletag.pubads().setTargeting('u', 's');
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting('compliant', module.adMap.compliant);

            googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
            googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
            googletag.pubads().setCentering(true);
            googletag.enableServices();

            /* prebid */
            if (typeof pbjs === 'undefined'
                || typeof window.epi_bidders === 'undefined'
                || module.epiCountBiddersDone >= window.epi_bidders) {
                module.log('La librería pb.js no está cargada, la variable `epi_bidders` no está definida o se ha llegado al número máximo de pujas. Se llama a `handleFirstAuctionEnd`.');
                module.handleFirstAuctionEnd();
            } else {
                var prebidTimeoutId = setTimeout(function () {
                    module.log('Han pasado 2 segundos sin que el número máximo de pujas se haya alcanzado. Se llama a `handleFirstAuctionEnd`.');
                    module.handleFirstAuctionEnd();
                    clearTimeout(prebidTimeoutId);
                }, FAILSAFE_TIMEOUT);
                pbjs.que.push(function () {
                    module.log('Escuchamos el evento `pbjs.que.bidderDone` para llamar a `handleFirstAuctionEnd` cuando se llegue al número máximo de pujas.');
                    pbjs.onEvent('bidderDone', function () {
                        module.log('`pbjs.que.bidderDone`');
                        if (module.epiCountBiddersDone >= window.epi_bidders) {
                            module.log('Se ha llegado al número máximo de pujas. Se llama a `handleFirstAuctionEnd`.');
                            module.handleFirstAuctionEnd();
                            clearTimeout(prebidTimeoutId);
                        }
                    });
                });
            }

            /* apstag */
            if (typeof apstag === 'undefined') {
                module.log('apstag no se ha cargado.');
                flags.set(flags.APSTAG_READY);
            } else if (apstagslots.length === 0) {
                module.log('No hay slots para apstag.');
                flags.set(flags.APSTAG_READY);
            } else {
                var apstagTimeoutId = setTimeout(function () {
                    module.log('Han pasado 2 segundos y apstag no ha termiando.');
                    flags.set(flags.APSTAG_READY);
                    clearTimeout(apstagTimeoutId);
                }, FAILSAFE_TIMEOUT);
                apstag.fetchBids({ slots: apstagslots }, function () {
                    apstag.setDisplayBids();
                    flags.set(flags.APSTAG_READY);
                    clearTimeout(apstagTimeoutId);
                });
            }
        }

        function startBiddingProcess() {
            if (module.hideAdsForSubscribers) {
                module.log('Se omite la carga de pb.js y apstag debido a que el usuario es suscriptor.');
                flags.set(flags.PREBID_LOADED | flags.APSTAG_LOADED);
                return;
            }

            if (!module.adMap.disablePrebidLoad) {
                window.pbjs = window.pbjs || { que: [] };
                window.hb_epi = module.adMap.adUnit.split('/')[0]
                    + '_' + (module.device)
                    + module.adMap.headerBiddingType
                    + (location.pathname === '/' ? '_portada' : '');

                pbjs.que.push(function () {
                    pbjs.onEvent('bidderDone', function () {
                        module.epiCountBiddersDone++;
                        module.log('Llamada a función `pbjs.onEvent:bidderDone`. Incrementando `epiCountBiddersDone`:', epiCountBiddersDone);
                    });
                });

                module.log('Iniciando el proceso de pujas con hb_epi: ', hb_epi);

                // Load Pbjs script
                var s = document.createElement('script');
                s.type = 'text/javascript';
                s.src = 'https://cdn3.richaudience.com/ab083674fb8200b877a6983126e4477d/prensaiberica/pb_wrapper/stage_2.js';
                s.async = true;
                s.onload = function () {
                    flags.set(flags.PREBID_LOADED);
                    module.log('prebid está listo para ser usado');
                };
                document.head.appendChild(s);
            } else {
                flags.set(flags.PREBID_LOADED);
                module.log('Se omite la carga de pb.js porque así fue indicado en el AdMap.');
            }

            if (!module.adMap.disableApstagLoad) {
                // Load Asptag script
                try {
